Where is?

code?

on github here

I have made four basic "shells" so far with gradually more (computationally expensive : slow) abstraction and power at each level: They are nested together like russian dolls ((4)abstract/big doll > (3) > (2) > (1)specific/bare bones/small doll).

  1. http://infoburp.com/index.html << the basic graph layout (very little abstraction "bare bones" graph)

  2. http://infoburp.com/about.html << a html page made with d3 elements (view interesting arrangements from small graph components and partial interaction)

  3. http://infoburp.com/script/google-closure-library/closure/goog/demos/editor/seamlessfield.html << a "semantiki"/"wysiwiki" (edit graph arrangements in line with viewing them)

  4. http://infoburp.com/threeshells.html <<1+2+3 on one screen (snail on a slow day on my netbook)

test my browser range
test my browser features
test my browser events
test my browser channels
